public class TestJobTagList {

        try {
            // Test JSON with tag_list field

                "\"status\": \"success\"" +
                "}";

# Read the original file
with open('/testbed/gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Add tagList field after project field
content = re.sub(r'(private Project project;)\n', r'\1\n    private List<String> tagList;\n', content)

# Add getter and setter methods after withProject method
pattern = r'(public Job withProject\(Project project\) \{\s*\n\s*this\.project = project;\s*\n\s*return this;\s*\n\s*\})(\s*\n)'
replacement = r'\1\n\n    public List<String> getTagList() {\n        return tagList;\n    }\n\n    public void setTagList(List<String> tagList) {\n        this.tagList = tagList;\n    }\n\n    public Job withTagList(List<String> tagList) {\n        this.tagList = tagList;\n        return this;\n    }\2'

content = re.sub(pattern, replacement, content)

# Write the modified content
with open('/testbed/gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("File modified successfully")

cd /testbed && cat > fix_job.py << 'EOF'
import re

# Read the original file
with open('gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Find the line with "private Project project;" and insert tagList after it
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if 'private Project project;' in line:
        lines.insert(i + 1, '    private List<String> tagList;\n')
        break

# Find the line with "public Job withProject(Project project) {" and insert methods after it
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if 'public Job withProject(Project project) {' in line:
        # Find the closing brace of this method (3 lines after)
        j = i
        while j < len(lines) and '}' not in lines[j]:
            j += 1
        
        # Insert the new methods after the closing brace
        new_methods = '''
    public List<String> getTagList() {
        return tagList;
    }

    public void setTagList(List<String> tagList) {
        this.tagList = tagList;
    }

    public Job withTagList(List<String> tagList) {
        this.tagList = tagList;
        return this;
    }
'''
        lines.insert(j + 1, new_methods)
        break

# Write the modified content back
with open('gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(lines)

print("Job.java has been successfully modified.")
EOF

cd /testbed && cat > add_taglist.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash

FILE="gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java"
BACKUP="$FILE.backup"
TEMP="$FILE.temp"

# Create a backup
cp "$FILE" "$BACKUP"

# Find line number with "private Project project;"
LINE_NUM=$(grep -n "private Project project;" "$FILE" | cut -d: -f1)

# Add tagList field after Project project
sed "${LINE_NUM}a\\n    private List<String> tagList;" "$FILE" > "$TEMP"
mv "$TEMP" "$FILE"

# Find line number with "withProject" method
LINE_NUM=$(grep -n "public Job withProject(Project project)" "$FILE" | cut -d: -f1)

# Add methods after withProject
sed "${LINE_NUM}a\\n    public List<String> getTagList() {\n        return tagList;\n    }\n\n    public void setTagList(List<String> tagList) {\n        this.tagList = tagList;\n    }\n\n    public Job withTagList(List<String> tagList) {\n        this.tagList = tagList;\n        return this;\n    }" "$FILE" > "$TEMP"
mv "$TEMP" "$FILE"

echo "Modified Job.java"
EOF

chmod +x add_taglist.sh
./add_taglist.sh

#!/bin/bash

# Restore from original
cp gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java.original gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java

# Insert the methods properly

echo "Job.java has been modified"
EOF

chmod +x manual_fix.sh
./manual_fix.sh

+            // Test JSON with tag_list field
+            String json = "{" +
+                "\"id\": 1," +
+                "\"name\": \"test-job\"," +
+                "\"tag_list\": [\"tag1\", \"tag2\", \"tag3\"]," +
+                "\"status\": \"success\"" +
+                "}";
+            
+            ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
+            Job job = mapper.readValue(json, Job.class);
+            
+            // Try to access tag_list field
+            try {
+                java.lang.reflect.Method getTagListMethod = Job.class.getMethod("getTagList");
+                Object tagList = getTagListMethod.invoke(job);
+                System.out.println("SUCCESS: tag_list field exists: " + tagList);
+            } catch (NoSuchMethodException e) {
+                System.out.println("ERROR: tag_list field is missing from Job class");
+                System.out.println("Expected: List<String> getTagList() method");
+            }
+            
+        } catch (Exception e) {
+            e.printStackTrace();
+        }
+    }
+}
diff --git a/add_taglist.sh b/add_taglist.sh
new file mode 100755
index 00000000..f67c51ba
--- /dev/null
+++ b/add_taglist.sh
@@ -0,0 +1,24 @@
+#!/bin/bash
+
+FILE="gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java"
+BACKUP="$FILE.backup"
+TEMP="$FILE.temp"
+
+# Create a backup
+cp "$FILE" "$BACKUP"
+
+# Find line number with "private Project project;"
+LINE_NUM=$(grep -n "private Project project;" "$FILE" | cut -d: -f1)
+
+# Add tagList field after Project project
+sed "${LINE_NUM}a\\n    private List<String> tagList;" "$FILE" > "$TEMP"
+mv "$TEMP" "$FILE"
+
+# Find line number with "withProject" method
+LINE_NUM=$(grep -n "public Job withProject(Project project)" "$FILE" | cut -d: -f1)
+
+# Add methods after withProject
+sed "${LINE_NUM}a\\n    public List<String> getTagList() {\n        return tagList;\n    }\n\n    public void setTagList(List<String> tagList) {\n        this.tagList = tagList;\n    }\n\n    public Job withTagList(List<String> tagList) {\n        this.tagList = tagList;\n        return this;\n    }" "$FILE" > "$TEMP"
+mv "$TEMP" "$FILE"
+
+echo "Modified Job.java"
diff --git a/fix_job.py b/fix_job.py
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..eb5c82bd
--- /dev/null
+++ b/fix_job.py
@@ -0,0 +1,43 @@
+import re
+
+# Read the original file
+with open('gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java', 'r') as f:
+    lines = f.readlines()
+
+# Find the line with "private Project project;" and insert tagList after it
+for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+    if 'private Project project;' in line:
+        lines.insert(i + 1, '    private List<String> tagList;\n')
+        break
+
+# Find the line with "public Job withProject(Project project) {" and insert methods after it
+for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+    if 'public Job withProject(Project project) {' in line:
+        # Find the closing brace of this method (3 lines after)
+        j = i
+        while j < len(lines) and '}' not in lines[j]:
+            j += 1
+        
+        # Insert the new methods after the closing brace
+        new_methods = '''
+    public List<String> getTagList() {
+        return tagList;
+    }
+
+    public void setTagList(List<String> tagList) {
+        this.tagList = tagList;
+    }
+
+    public Job withTagList(List<String> tagList) {
+        this.tagList = tagList;
+        return this;
+    }
+'''
+        lines.insert(j + 1, new_methods)
+        break
+
+# Write the modified content back
+with open('gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java', 'w') as f:
+    f.writelines(lines)
+
+print("Job.java has been successfully modified.")

+#!/bin/bash
+
+# Restore original
+cp gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java.original gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java
+
+# Add tagList field
+sed -i '/private Project project;/a\\n    private List<String> tagList;' gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java
+
+# Find the position to insert methods - after withProject
+LINE=$(grep -n "public Job withProject" gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java | cut -d: -f1)
+# Add 3 lines to get past the closing brace
+INSERT_POS=$((LINE + 3))
+
+# Create a temporary file with the new content
+head -n $INSERT_POS gitlab4j-models/src/main/java/org/gitlab4j/api/models/Job.java > /tmp/job_temp.java
+
+# Add the new methods
+cat >> /tmp/job_temp.java << 'EOF'
+
+    public List<String> getTagList() {
+        return tagList;
+    }
+
+    public void setTagList(List<String> tagList) {
+        this.tagList = tagList;
+    }
+
+    public Job withTagList(List<String> tagList) {
+        this.tagList = tagList;
+        return this;
+    }

+        this.queuedDuration = queuedDuration;
+        return this;
+    }
+
+    public Job withProject(Project project) {
+        this.project = project;
+        return this;
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    public String toString() {
+        return (JacksonJson.toJsonString(this));
+    }
+}
